<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ворчливый.html>ворчли́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vorčlívyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ворчли́вее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ворчли́вей</b>)

***восвояси.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:восвояси.html>восвоя́си</a> (15724)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">въ своѩ <a href = vnd.unilang:си.html>си</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vŭ svoję si</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восвояси.html>восвоя́си</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vosvojási</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> back (to the original place, where one came from); homewards, homeward, home</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:восвояси.html>восвоя́си</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:наречие.html>Наре́чие</a>; неизменяемое.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-восвояси-</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

***восемнадцать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:восемнадцать.html>восемна́дцать</a> (4768)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compounded from <b><a href = vnd.unilang:восемь.html>восемь</a></b> + <b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b> + <b>дцать</b>, or <i>eight on ten</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восемнадцать.html>восемна́дцать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vosemnádcatʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>eighteen (18)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:восемнадцать.html>восемна́дцать</a></strong></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vosemnadcatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in the nominative case and accusative case governs the genitive plural of the noun. In other cases, it governs the corresponding plural case of the noun.
</p>
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:восемнадцать.html>восемна́дцать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vosemnádcatʹ</b> málʹčikov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">eighteen boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:восемнадцать.html>восемна́дцатью</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиками</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>vosemnádcatʹju</b> málʹčikami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">with eighteen boys</span></div></li>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:сей.html>сем</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>на́д</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>цать</b>
</p><p>Числительное, <a href = vnd.unilang:количественный.html>коли́чественное</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:порядковый.html>поря́дковое</a> числительное — <a href = vnd.unilang:восемнадцатый.html>восемна́дцатый</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-восем-</b>; суффикс: <b>-надцать</b>.
</p>

***восемь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:восемь.html>восемь</a> (1167)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*osmь</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*oḱtṓw</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восемь.html>во́семь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vósemʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>eight (8)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:восемь.html>восемь</a></strong></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vosemʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in the nominative case and accusative case governs the genitive plural of the noun. In other cases, it governs the corresponding plural case of the noun.
</p>
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:восемь.html>во́семь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vósemʹ</b> málʹčikov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">eight boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:восемь.html>восемью́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиками</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>vosemʹjú</b> málʹčikami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">with eight boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:восемь.html>во́семь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">málʹčikov <b>vósemʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">approximately eight boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пятьдесят.html>пятьдеся́т</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:восемь.html>во́семь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́г</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pjatʹdesját <b>vósemʹ</b> knig</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fifty-eight books</span></div></li></ul>

***восемьдесят.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:восемьдесят.html>во́семьдесят</a> (4233)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compounded from <b><a href = vnd.unilang:восемь.html>восемь</a></b> + <b><a href = vnd.unilang:десять.html>де́сять</a></b>, or <i>eight tens</i>. <b>Десят</b> was the <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span></span> genitive plural, which is required by numbers <a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a> and up.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восемьдесят.html>во́семьдесят</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vósemʹdesjat</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>eighty (80)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:восемьдесят.html>во́семьдесят</a></strong></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vosemʹdesjat</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in the nominative case and accusative case governs the genitive plural of the noun. In other cases, it governs the corresponding plural case of the noun.
</p>
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:восемьдесят.html>во́семьдесят</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vósemʹdesjat</b> málʹčikov</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>eighty</b> boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:восемьдесят.html>восемью́десятью</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиками</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>vosemʹjúdesjatʹju</b> málʹčikami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">with <b>eighty</b> boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:восемьдесят.html>во́семьдесят</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">málʹčikov <b>vósemʹdesjat</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">approximately <b>eighty</b> boys</span></div></li></ul>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восклицание.html>восклица́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vosklicánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восклицание.html>восклица́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восклицание.html>восклица́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восклицание.html>восклица́ний</a></b>)

***воскресенье.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:воскресенье.html>воскресе́нье</a> (2749)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воскресение.html>воскресе́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">voskresénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воскрешение.html>воскреше́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">voskrešénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (resurrection, of Christ).
</p><p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>День</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:воскрешение.html>воскреше́ния</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Denʹ voskrešénija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (The Day of Resurrection) means a holiday, a nonworking day, and in this meaning it replaced the word <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неделя.html>неде́ля</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nedélja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> which had been used for Sunday before.
</p><p>Compare with Old East Slavic and Old Church Slavonic <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">въскрьсениѥ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vŭskrĭsenije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">въскрѣшениѥ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vŭskrěšenije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Because of the prefix <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вос-</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vos-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (rather than <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вс-</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vs-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), it was an adoption from Old Church Slavonic (not Old Slavonic).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воскресенье.html>воскресе́нье</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">voskresénʹje</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воскресенье.html>воскресе́нья</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воскресенье.html>воскресе́нья</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воскресенье.html>воскресе́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Sunday
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:воскресенье.html>воскресе́нье</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>voskresénʹje</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">on Sunday</span></div></dd>

***воскресить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:воскресить.html>воскреси́ть</a> (20165)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воскреснуть.html>воскре́снуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voskrésnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воскресить.html>воскреси́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">voskresítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воскрешать.html>воскреша́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to raise from the dead, to resurrect</li>
<li>to revive, to resuscitate, to reanimate</li>
<li>to revive, to recall, to call up, to bring back
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:воскресить.html>воскреси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:память.html>па́мяти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>voskresítʹ</b> v pámjati</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to conjure up (bring back) the memory (of)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воскресение.html>воскресе́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">voskresénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p>Compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воскресить.html>воскреси́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voskresítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to resurrect</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воскреснуть.html>воскре́снуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">voskrésnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">воскреса́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to revive, to resurrect, to rise from the dead</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to revive, to feel reanimated, to rise again</li>
<li><i>(feelings, images etc.)</i> to revive, to come back
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:воскреснуть.html>воскре́снуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:память.html>па́мяти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>voskrésnutʹ</b> v pámjati</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to come back (recur) to one's memory</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:воскрешать.html>воскреша́ть</a> (26272)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воскресить.html>воскреси́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voskresítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воскрешать.html>воскреша́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">voskrešátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воскресить.html>воскреси́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to raise from the dead</li>
<li>to revive, to resuscitate, to reanimate</li>
<li>to revive, to recall, to call up, to bring back
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:воскрешать.html>воскреша́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:память.html>па́мяти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>voskrešátʹ</b> v pámjati</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to conjure up (bring back) the memory (of)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
